!important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;bar<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">:</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"hello"</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">令人惊讶的是，这两个函数不会返回相同的结果。而是：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"foo1 returns:"</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">foo1</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"foo2 returns:"</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">foo2</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">会产生：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">foo1 returns<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">:</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">Object&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span>bar<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">:</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"hello"</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">foo2 returns<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">:</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">undefined</p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">这不仅令人惊讶，而且特别令人烦恼的是，foo2()返回未定义而没有引发任何错误。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">原因与JavaScript中分号在技术上是可选的事实有关（尽管忽略它们通常是非常糟糕的形式）。因此，在foo2()中遇到包含return语句的行（没有其他内容）时，
            <em style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">会在return语句之后立即自动插入分号。</em>
        </p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">由于代码的其余部分是完全有效的，即使它没有被调用或做任何事情（它只是一个未使用的代码块，它定义了一个属性栏，它等于字符串“hello”），所以不会抛出任何错误。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">这种行为也被认为是遵循了在JavaScript中将一行开头大括号放在行尾的约定，而不是在新行的开头。如此处所示，这不仅仅是JavaScript中的一种风格偏好。</p>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">7、什么是NaN？它的类型是什么？如何可靠地测试一个值是否等于NaN？</h3>
        <p style="margin-top: 8px;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">NaN属性表示“不是数字”的值。这个特殊值是由于一个操作数是非数字的（例如“abc”/ 4）或者因为操作的结果是非数字而无法执行的。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">虽然这看起来很简单，但NaN有一些令人惊讶的特征，如果人们没有意识到这些特征，就会导致bug。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">一方面，虽然NaN的意思是“不是数字”，但它的类型是，数字：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">typeof</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">NaN</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">===</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"number"</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" spellcheck="true" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(153, 153, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// logs "true"</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">此外，NaN相比任何事情 - 甚至本身！ - 是false：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">NaN</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">===</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">NaN</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" spellcheck="true" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(153, 153, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// logs "false"</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">测试数字是否等于NaN的半可靠方法是使用内置函数isNaN()，但即使使用 isNaN()也不是一个好的解决方案。.</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">一个更好的解决方案要么是使用value!==值，如果该值等于NaN，那么只会生成true。另外，ES6提供了一个新的Number.isNaN()函数 ，它与旧的全局isNaN()函数不同，也更加可靠。</p>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">8、下面的代码输出什么？解释你的答案。</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0.1</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0.2</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0.1</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0.2</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">==</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0.3</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">对这个问题的一个有教养的回答是：“你不能确定。它可能打印出0.3和true，或者可能不打印。 JavaScript中的数字全部用浮点精度处理，因此可能不会总是产生预期的结果。“</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">上面提供的示例是演示此问题的经典案例。令人惊讶的是，它会打印出来：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0.30000000000000004</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">false</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">一个典型的解决方案是比较两个数字与特殊常数Number.EPSILON之间的绝对差值：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">areTheNumbersAlmostEqual</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>num1<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;num2<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">return</span>&nbsp;Math<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">abs</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>&nbsp;num1&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">-</span>&nbsp;num2&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">&lt;</span>&nbsp;Number<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span>EPSILON<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">areTheNumbersAlmostEqual</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0.1</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0.2</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0.3</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">讨论写函数的可能方法isInteger(x)，它确定x是否是一个整数。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">这听起来很平凡，事实上，ECMAscript 6为此正好引入了一个新的Number.isInteger()函数，这是微不足道的。但是，在ECMAScript 6之前，这有点复杂，因为没有提供与Number.isInteger()方法等价的方法。</p>
        <p
            style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">问题在于，在ECMAScript规范中，整数只在概念上存在;即数值始终作为浮点值存储。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">考虑到这一点，最简单，最清洁的ECMAScript-6之前的解决方案（即使将非数字值（例如字符串或空值）传递给该函数，该解决方案也具有足够的可靠性以返回false）将成为以下用法按位异或运算符：</p>
        <blockquote
            class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">isInteger</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>x<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">return</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>x&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">^</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">===</span>&nbsp;x<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">下面的解决方案也可以工作，尽管不如上面那样高雅</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">isInteger</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>x<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">return</span>&nbsp;Math<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">round</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>x<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">===</span>&nbsp;x<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">请注意，在上面的实现中Math.ceil()或Math.floor()可以同样使用（而不是Math.round()）。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">或者：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">isInteger</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>x<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">return</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">typeof</span>&nbsp;x&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">===</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">'number'</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">&amp;&amp;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>x&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">%</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">===</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">一个相当常见的不正确的解决方案如下：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">isInteger</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>x<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">return</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">parseInt</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>x<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">10</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">===</span>&nbsp;x<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">虽然这个基于parseInt的方法对许多x值很有效，但一旦x变得相当大，它将无法正常工作。问题是parseInt()在解析数字之前将其第一个参数强制转换为字符串。因此，一旦数字变得足够大，其字符串表示将以指数形式呈现（例如1e
            + 21）。因此，parseInt()将尝试解析1e + 21，但是当它到达e字符时将停止解析，因此将返回值1.观察：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">&gt;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">String</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1000000000000000000000</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">'1e+21'</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word         </blockquote>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1000000000000000000000</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">false</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">9、执行下面的代码时，按什么顺序将数字1-4记录到控制台？为什么？</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">这些值将按以下顺序记录：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">4</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">3</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">我们先来解释一下这些可能更为明显的部分：</p>
        <ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="">
            <li>
                <p style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">首先显示1和4，因为它们是通过简单调用console.log()而没有任何延迟记录的</p>
                <p style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">
                    <br style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">
                </p>
            </li>
            <li>
                <p style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">在3之后显示，因为在延迟1000毫秒（即1秒）之后记录2，而在0毫秒的延迟之后记录3。</p>
                <p style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">
                    <br style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">
                </p>
            </li>
        </ul>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">好的。但是，如果在延迟0毫秒后记录3，这是否意味着它正在被立即记录？而且，如果是这样，不应该在4之前记录它，因为4是由后面的代码行记录的吗？</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">答案与正确理解JavaScript事件和时间有关。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">浏览器有一个事件循环，它检查事件队列并处理未决事件。例如，如果在浏览器繁忙时（例如，处理onclick）在后台发生事件（例如脚本onload事件），则该事件被附加到队列中。当onclick处理程序完成时，将检查队列并处理该事件（例如，执行onload脚本）。</p>
        <p
            style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">同样，如果浏览器繁忙，setTimeout()也会将其引用函数的执行放入事件队列中。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">当值为零作为setTimeout()的第二个参数传递时，它将尝试“尽快”执行指定的函数。具体来说，函数的执行放置在事件队列中，以在下一个计时器滴答时发生。但请注意，这不是直接的;该功能不会执行，直到下一个滴答声。这就是为什么在上面的例子中，调用console.log(4)发生在调用console.log(3)之前（因为调用console.log(3)是通过setTimeout调用的，所以稍微延迟了一点）。</p>
        <h3
            style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">10、编写一个简单的函数（少于160个字符），返回一个布尔值，指示字符串是否是palindrome。</h3>
        <p style="margin-top: 8px;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">如果str是回文，以下一行函数将返回true;否则，它返回false。</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>str<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;str&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">replace</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">''</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width:         </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">例如：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// logs 'true'</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap:
