!important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">isPalindrome</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"levels"</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" spellcheck="true" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(153, 153, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// logs 'false'</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">isPalindrome</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"A car, a man, a maraca"</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" spellcheck="true" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(153, 153, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// logs 'true'</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">11、写一个sum方法，当使用下面的语法调用时它将正常工作。</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">sum</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">3</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" spellcheck="true" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(153, 153, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// Outputs 5</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">sum</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">3</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" spellcheck="true" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(153, 153, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// Outputs 5</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">有（至少）两种方法可以做到这一点：</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <strong style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">METHOD 1</strong>
        </p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">if</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>arguments<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span>length&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">==</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">return</span>&nbsp;arguments<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">]</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;arguments<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">]</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">else</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">return</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span><span class="" style="max-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">return</span>&nbsp;x&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;y<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">在JavaScript中，函数提供对参数对象的访问，该对象提供对传递给函数的实际参数的访问。这使我们能够使用length属性在运行时确定传递给函数的参数的数量</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">如果传递两个参数，我们只需将它们相加并返回。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">否则，我们假设它是以sum(2)(3)的形式被调用的，所以我们返回一个匿名函数，它将传递给sum()（在本例中为2）的参数和传递给匿名函数的参数（这种情况3）。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <strong style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">METHOD 2</strong>
        </p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">sum</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>x<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;y<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">if</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>y&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">!==</span>&nbsp;undefined<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">return</span>&nbsp;x&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;y<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">else</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">return</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>y<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">return</span>&nbsp;x&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;y<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">当函数被调用时，JavaScript不需要参数的数量来匹配函数定义中参数的数量。如果传递的参数数量超过了函数定义中参数的数量，则超出的参数将被忽略。另一方面，如果传递的参数数量少于函数定义中的参数数量，则在函数内引用时，缺少的参数将具有未定义的值。因此，在上面的例子中，通过简单地检查第二个参数是否未定义，我们可以确定函数被调用的方式并相应地继续。</p>
        <h3
            style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">12、考虑下面的代码片段</h3>

        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">(a) 当用户点击“按钮4”时，什么被记录到控制台？为什么？</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">(b) 提供一个或多个可按预期工作的替代实现。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">答：</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">(a) 无论用户点击哪个按钮，数字5将始终记录到控制台。这是因为，在调用onclick方法（对于任何按钮）时，for循环已经完成，并且变量i已经具有值5.（如果受访者知道足够的话就可以获得奖励点数关于执行上下文，变量对象，激活对象和内部“范围”属性如何影响闭包行为。）</p>
        <p
            style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">(b) 使这项工作的关键是通过将它传递给新创建的函数对象来捕获每次通过for循环的i的值。以下是四种可能的方法来实现这一点：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">for</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;i&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">&lt;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;btn<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box         </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">或者，您可以将新的匿名函数中的整个调用包装为btn.addEventListener：</p>

!important;">(</span>btn<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">或者，我们可以通过调用数组对象的原生forEach方法来替换for循环：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">'b'</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;">(</span>value<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;i<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word         </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">最后，最简单的解决方案，如果你在ES6 / ES2015上下文中，就是使用let i而不是var i：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">

        </blockquote>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">13、假设d是范围内的“空”对象：</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;d&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">使用下面的代码完成了什么？</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">'zebra'</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span>k<span class="" style="max-width: style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">上面显示的代码片段在对象d上设置了两个属性。理想情况下，对具有未设置键的JavaScript对象执行的查找评估为未定义。但是运行这段代码会将这些属性标记为对象的“自己的属性”。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">这是确保对象具有一组给定属性的有用策略。将该对象传递给Object.keys将返回一个包含这些设置键的数组（即使它们的值未定义）。</p>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">14、下面的代码将输出到控制台，为什么？</h3>

100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"array 2: length="</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;arr2<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span>length&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">" last="</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;arr2<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">slice</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">-</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">记录的输出将是：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"array 1: length=5 last=j,o,n,e,s"</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"array 2: length=5 last=j,o,n,e,s"</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">arr1和arr2是相同的（即['n'，'h'，'o'，'j'，['j'，'o'，'n'，'e'，'s']]）上述代码由于以下原因而被执行：</p>
        <ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="">
            <li>
                <p style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">调用数组对象的reverse()方法不仅以相反的顺序返回数组，它还颠倒了数组本身的顺序（即在这种情况下，arr1）。</p>
                <p style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">
                    <br style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">
                </p>
            </li>
            <li>
                <p style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">reverse()方法返回对数组本身的引用（即，在这种情况下为arr1）。因此，arr2仅仅是对arr1的引用（而不是副本）。因此，当对arr2做任何事情时（即，当我们调用arr2.push(arr3);）时，arr1也会受到影响，因为arr1和arr2只是对同一个对象的引用。</p>
                <p
                    style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">
                    <br style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">
                </p>
            </li>
        </ul>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">这里有几个观点可以让人们回答这个问题：</p>
        <ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="">
            <li>
                <p style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">将数组传递给另一个数组的push()方法会将整个数组作为单个元素推入数组的末尾。结果，声明arr2.push(arr3);将arr3作为一个整体添加到arr2的末尾（即，它不连接两个数组，这就是concat()方法的用途）。</p>
                <p
                    style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">
                    <br style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">
                </p>
            </li>
            <li>
                <p style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">像Python一样，JavaScript在调用像slice()这样的数组方法时，会承认负面下标，以此作为在数组末尾引用元素的方式;例如，下标-1表示数组中的最后一个元素，依此类推。</p>
                <p style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">
                    <br style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">
                </p>
            </li>
        </ul>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">15、下面的代码将输出到控制台，为什么？</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"B"</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">以上代码将输出到控制台：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"122"</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"32"</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"02"</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"112"</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"NaN2"</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">NaN</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">这是为什么...</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">这里的基本问题是JavaScript（ECMAScript）是一种松散类型的语言，它对值执行自动类型转换以适应正在执行的操作。让我们来看看这是如何与上面的每个例子进行比较。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">示例1：1 +“2”+“2”输出：“122”说明：第一个操作在1 +“2”中执行。由于其中一个操作数（“2”）是一个字符串，所以JavaScript假定需要执行字符串连接，因此将1的类型转换为“1”，1 +“2”转换为“12”。然后，“12”+“2”产生“122”。</p>
        <p
            style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">示例2：1 + +“2”+“2”输出：“32”说明：根据操作顺序，要执行的第一个操作是+“2”（第一个“2”之前的额外+被视为一个一元运算符）。因此，JavaScript将“2”的类型转换为数字，然后将一元+符号应用于它（即将其视为正数）。结果，下一个操作现在是1
            + 2，当然这会产生3.但是，我们有一个数字和一个字符串之间的操作（即3和“2”），所以JavaScript再次转换数值赋给一个字符串并执行字符串连接，产生“32”。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">示例3：1 + - “1”+“2”输出：“02”说明：这里的解释与前面的示例相同，只是一元运算符是 - 而不是+。因此，“1”变为1，然后在应用 - 时将其变为-1，然后将其加1到产生0，然后转换为字符串并与最终的“2”操作数连接，产生“02”。</p>
        <p
            style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">示例4：+“1”+“1”+“2”输出：“112”说明：尽管第一个“1”操作数是基于其前面的一元+运算符的数值类型转换的，当它与第二个“1”操作数连接在一起时返回一个字符串，然后与最终的“2”操作数连接，产生字符串“112”。</p>
        <p
            style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">示例5：“A” - “B”+“2”输出：“NaN2”说明：由于 - 运算符不能应用于字符串，并且既不能将“A”也不能将“B”转换为数值， “ - ”B“产生NaN，然后与字符串”2“串联产生”NaN2“。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">例6：“A” - “B”+2输出：NaN说明：在前面的例子中，“A” - “B”产生NaN。但是任何运算符应用于NaN和其他数字操作数仍然会产生NaN。</p>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">16、如果数组列表太大，以下递归代码将导致堆栈溢出。你如何解决这个问题，仍然保留递归模式？</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45,         </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">通过修改nextListItem函数可以避免潜在的堆栈溢出，如下所示：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;list&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;item&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;list<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">pop</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 0;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;height: 6px;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><br style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">if</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>item<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" spellcheck="true" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(153, 153, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// process the list item...</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">setTimeout</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>&nbsp;nextListItem<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">堆栈溢出被消除，因为事件循环处理递归，而不是调用堆栈。当nextListItem运行时，如果item不为null，则将超时函数（nextListItem）推送到事件队列，并且函数退出，从而使调用堆栈清零。当事件队列运行超时事件时，将处理下一个项目，并设置一个计时器以再次调用nextListItem。因此，该方法从头到尾不经过直接递归调用即可处理，因此调用堆栈保持清晰，无论迭代次数如何。</p>
        <h3
            style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">17、什么是JavaScript中的“闭包”？举一个例子。</h3>
        <p style="margin-top: 8px;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">闭包是一个内部函数，它可以访问外部（封闭）函数的作用域链中的变量。闭包可以访问三个范围内的变量;具体来说： （1）变量在其自己的范围内， （2）封闭函数范围内的变量 （3）全局变量。
        </p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">这里是一个例子：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;globalVar&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"xyz"</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 0;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;height: 6px;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><br style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">outerFunc</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>outerArg<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;outerVar&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 6px;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><br style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: !important;">"\n"</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"\n"</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"innerVar = "</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;innerVar&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"\n"</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">"globalVar = "</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">+</span>&nbsp;globalVar<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 0;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;height: 6px;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><br style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color:         </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">在上面的例子中，innerFunc，outerFunc和全局名称空间的变量都在innerFunc的范围内。上面的代码将产生以下输出：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">globalVar&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;xyz</p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">18、以下代码的输出是什么：</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45,
