        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">解释你的答案。如何在这里使用闭包？</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">显示的代码示例不会显示值0,1,2,3和4，这可能是预期的;而是显示5,5,5,5。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">这是因为循环内执行的每个函数将在整个循环完成后执行，因此所有函数都会引用存储在i中的最后一个值，即5。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">通过为每次迭代创建一个唯一的作用域，可以使用闭包来防止这个问题，并将该变量的每个唯一值存储在其作用域中，如下所示：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">for</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;i&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;i&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">&lt;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;i<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: !important;">,</span>&nbsp;x&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1000</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>i<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">这会产生将0,1,2,3和4记录到控制台的可能结果。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">在ES2015上下文中，您可以在原始代码中简单地使用let而不是var：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45,         </blockquote>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">19、以下几行代码输出到控制台？</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45,         <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">解释你的答案。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">该代码将输出以下四行：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">&amp;&amp;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">0</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">&amp;&amp;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">在JavaScript中，都是||和&amp;&amp;是逻辑运算符，当从左向右计算时返回第一个完全确定的“逻辑值”。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">或（||）运算符。在形式为X || Y的表达式中，首先计算X并将其解释为布尔值。如果此布尔值为真，则返回true（1），并且不计算Y，因为“或”条件已经满足。但是，如果此布尔值为“假”，我们仍然不知道X || Y是真还是假，直到我们评估Y，并将其解释为布尔值。</p>
        <p
            style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">因此，0 || 1评估为真（1），正如1 || 2。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">和（&amp;&amp;）运算符。在X &amp;&amp; Y形式的表达式中，首先评估X并将其解释为布尔值。如果此布尔值为false，则返回false（0）并且不评估Y，因为“and”条件已失败。但是，如果这个布尔值为“真”，我们仍然不知道X
            &amp;&amp; Y是真还是假，直到我们评估Y，并将其解释为布尔值。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">然而，&amp;&amp;运算符的有趣之处在于，当表达式评估为“真”时，则返回表达式本身。这很好，因为它在逻辑表达式中被视为“真”，但也可以用于在您关心时返回该值。这解释了为什么，有点令人惊讶的是，1 &amp;&amp; 2返回2（而你可能会期望它返回true或1）。</p>
        <h3
            style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">20 、下面的代码执行时输出是什么？说明。</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">false</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">==</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">'0'</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">false</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">===</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">'0'</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">该代码将输出：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">true</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">false</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">在JavaScript中，有两套相等运算符。三重相等运算符===的行为与任何传统的相等运算符相同：如果两侧的两个表达式具有相同的类型和相同的值，则计算结果为true。然而，双等号运算符在比较它们之前试图强制这些值。因此，通常使用===而不是==。对于！==
            vs！=也是如此。</p>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">21、以下代码的输出是什么？解释你的答案。</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, !important;">,</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;b<span class="" 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">'b'</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;c<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span>key<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">a<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">]</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">a<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span>c<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">]</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">456</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 0;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;height: 6px;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><br style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>a<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span>b<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">]</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">此代码的输出将是456（不是123）。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">原因如下：设置对象属性时，JavaScript会隐式地将参数值串联起来。在这种情况下，由于b和c都是对象，它们都将被转换为“[object Object]”。因此，a [b]和a [c]都等价于[“[object Object]”]，并且可以互换使用。因此，设置或引用[c]与设置或引用[b]完全相同。</p>
        <h3
            style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">22、以下代码将输出到控制台中.</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box break-word !important;">return</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>n&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">&gt;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">?</span>&nbsp;n&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">*</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">f</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>n<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">-1</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">:</span>&nbsp;n<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">该代码将输出10阶乘的值（即10！或3,628,800）。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">原因如下：</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">命名函数f()以递归方式调用自身，直到它调用f(1)，它简单地返回1.因此，这就是它的作用：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45,         </blockquote>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">23 、考虑下面的代码片段。控制台的输出是什么，为什么？</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" !important;">)</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>x<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span><span class="" style="max-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">输出将为1，即使x的值从未在内部函数中设置。原因如下：</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">正如我们的JavaScript招聘指南中所解释的，闭包是一个函数，以及创建闭包时在范围内的所有变量或函数。在JavaScript中，闭包被实现为“内部函数”;即在另一功能的主体内定义的功能。闭包的一个重要特征是内部函数仍然可以访问外部函数的变量。</p>
        <p
            style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">因此，在这个例子中，因为x没有在内部函数中定义，所以在外部函数的作用域中搜索一个定义的变量x，该变量的值为1。</p>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">24、以下代码将输出到控制台以及为什么</h3>

initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width:         </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">这段代码有什么问题，以及如何解决这个问题。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">该代码将输出：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">undefined</p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">John Doe</p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">第一个console.log打印未定义，因为我们从hero对象中提取方法，所以stoleSecretIdentity()在_name属性不存在的全局上下文（即窗口对象）中被调用。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">修复stoleSecretIdentity()函数的一种方法如下：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;stoleSecretIdentity&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;hero<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span>getSecretIdentity<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">bind</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>hero<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">25、创建一个函数，给定页面上的DOM元素，将访问元素本身及其所有后代（
            <em style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;font-size: inherit !important;">不仅仅是它的直接子元素</em>）。对于每个访问的元素，函数应该将该元素传递给提供的回调函数。</h3>
        <p style="margin-top: 8px;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">该函数的参数应该是：</p>
        <ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="">
            <li>
                <p style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">一个 DOM 元素</p>
            </li>
            <li>
                <p style="max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.9;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;">一个回调函数（以DOM元素作为参数）</p>
            </li>
        </ul>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">访问树中的所有元素（DOM）是经典的深度优先搜索算法应用程序。以下是一个示例解决方案：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">Traverse</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;p_element<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span>children<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word         </blockquote>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">27、在JavaScript中测试您的这些知识：以下代码的输出是什么？</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;length&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">10</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">fn</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;arguments<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 0;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;height: 6px;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><br style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">obj<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">method</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>fn<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">输出：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">10</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">为什么不是10和5？</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">首先，由于fn作为函数方法的参数传递，函数fn的作用域（this）是窗口。 var length = 10;在窗口级别声明。它也可以作为window.length或length或this.length来访问（当这个===窗口时）。</p>
        <p
            style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">方法绑定到Object obj，obj.method用参数fn和1调用。虽然方法只接受一个参数，但调用它时已经传递了两个参数;第一个是函数回调，其他只是一个数字。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">当在内部方法中调用fn()时，该函数在全局级别作为参数传递，this.length将有权访问在Object obj中定义的var length = 10（全局声明）而不是length = 5。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">现在，我们知道我们可以使用arguments []数组访问JavaScript函数中的任意数量的参数。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">因此arguments0只不过是调用fn()。在fn里面，这个函数的作用域成为参数数组，并且记录参数[]的长度将返回2。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">因此输出将如上所述。</p>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">28、考虑下面的代码。输出是什么，为什么？</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style:         </blockquote>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">undefined</p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">var语句被挂起（没有它们的值初始化）到它所属的全局或函数作用域的顶部，即使它位于with或catch块内。但是，错误的标识符只在catch块内部可见。它相当于：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45,         <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">29、这段代码的输出是什么？</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;x&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">21</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;girl&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>x<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;x&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">20</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">girl&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">21，也不是20，结果是‘undefined’的</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">这是因为JavaScript初始化没有被挂起。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">（为什么它不显示21的全局值？原因是当函数执行时，它检查是否存在本地x变量但尚未声明它，因此它不会查找全局变量。）</p>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">30、你如何克隆一个对象？</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>b<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">:</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;Object<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">assign</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">{</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>obj<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">现在objclone的值是{a：1，b：2}，但指向与obj不同的对象。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">但请注意潜在的缺陷：Object.clone()只会执行浅拷贝，而不是深拷贝。这意味着嵌套的对象不会被复制。他们仍然引用与原始相同的嵌套对象：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45,         </blockquote>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">31、此代码将打印什么？</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45,         </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">它会打印0 1 2 3 4，因为我们在这里使用let而不是var。变量i只能在for循环的块范围中看到。</p>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">32、以下几行输出什么，为什么？</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45,         </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">第一条语句返回true，如预期的那样。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">第二个返回false是因为引擎如何针对&lt;和&gt;的操作符关联性工作。它比较从左到右，所以3&gt; 2&gt; 1 JavaScript翻译为true&gt; 1. true具有值1，因此它比较1&gt; 1，这是错误的。</p>
        <h3
            style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">33、如何在数组的开头添加元素？最后如何添加一个？</h3>
