100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>myArray<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" spellcheck="true" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(153, 153, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// ["start", "a", "b", "c", "d", "end"]</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">使用ES6，可以使用扩展运算符：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">myArray&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">'start'</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">...</span>myArray<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">]</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">myArray&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">...</span>myArray<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">'end'</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">]</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">或者，简而言之：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">myArray&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">'start'</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">...</span>myArray<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(126, 198, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">'end'</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">]</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">34、想象一下你有这样的代码:</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;a&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">,</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">3</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">]</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">a）这会导致崩溃吗？</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">a<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">10</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">]</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">99</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">b）这个输出是什么？</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box break-word !important;">(</span>a<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">6</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">]</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">a）它不会崩溃。 JavaScript引擎将使阵列插槽3至9成为“空插槽”。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">b）在这里，a [6]将输出未定义的值，但时隙仍为空，而不是未定义的。在某些情况下，这可能是一个重要的细微差别。例如，使用map()时，map()的输出中的空插槽将保持为空，但未定义的插槽将使用传递给它的函数重映射：</p>
        <blockquote
            class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;b&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">[</span>undefined<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">]</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">b<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>b<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" spellcheck="true" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(153, 153, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// (3) [undefined, empty × 1, 1]</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>b<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">map</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>e&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">&gt;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" spellcheck="true" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(153, 153, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// (3) [7, empty × 1, 7]</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">35、typeof undefined == typeof NULL的值是什么？</h3>
        <p style="margin-top: 8px;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">该表达式将被评估为true，因为NULL将被视为任何其他未定义的变量。</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding-top: 10px;padding-right: 10px;padding-bottom: 10px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <p style="padding-right: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 1.7;text-align: justify;white-space: pre-wrap;word-break: break-all;text-overflow: ellipsis;overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box !important;">注意：JavaScript区分大小写，我们在这里使用NULL而不是null。</p>
        </blockquote>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">36、代码返回后会怎么样？</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">typeof</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">typeof</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">打印结果：string</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">typeof 1将返回“number”，typeof“number”将返回字符串。</p>
        <h3 style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;padding-left: 25px;font-weight: bold;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;">37、以下代码输出什么？为什么？</h3>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, 45, 45);color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;"><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;b&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;b&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">inner</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: break-word !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;b<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: break-word !important;">)</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">outer</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">输出到控制台将是“3”。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">在这个例子中有三个闭包，每个都有它自己的var b声明。当调用变量时，将按照从本地到全局的顺序检查闭包，直到找到实例。由于内部闭包有自己的b变量，这就是输出。</p>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">此外，由于提升内部的代码将被解释如下：</p>
        <blockquote class="" style="padding-left: 0px;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">
            <pre class="" style="margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em;max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;overflow: auto;background-color: rgb(45, break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">function</span>&nbsp;inner&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;">{</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(204, 153, 205);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">var</span>&nbsp;b<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// b is undefined</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;b<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">++</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" spellcheck="true" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(153, 153, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// b is NaN</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;b&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(103, 205, 204);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">=</span>&nbsp;<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">3</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" spellcheck="true" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(153, 153, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// b is 3</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;console<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">.</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(240, 141, 73);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">log</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">(</span>b<span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">)</span><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">;</span>&nbsp;<span class="" spellcheck="true" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;color: rgb(153, 153, 153);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">// output "3"</span></p><p class="" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-bottom: 3px;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;line-height: 16px;font-size: 12px;text-align: justify;word-break: break-all;box-sizing: border-box !important;white-space: nowrap !important;"><span class="" style="max-width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;">}</span></p></pre>
        </blockquote>
        <p style="margin-top: 1.8em;margin-bottom: 1.8em;max-width: 100%;word-wrap: break-word;min-height: 1em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">面试比棘手的技术问题要多，所以这些仅仅是作为指导。并不是每个值得聘用的“A”候选人都能够回答所有问题，能够回答所有问题的也不能保证是“A”候选人。最后，招聘仍然是一门艺术，一门科学 - 还有很多工作要做。</p>
        <p>
            <br>
        </p>

        })();

    <div class="ct_mpda_wrp" id="js_sponsor_ad_area" style="display:none;"></div>
</div>
